## Instruction

Please help me prepare a graduate application report for a student currently living in Los Angeles, California, who wishes to attend a nearby university to be able to return home regularly. Please help me find detailed information about all schools within 500 miles of the Natural History Museum of Los Angeles County that are ranked in the top 30 in the CS Ranking AI field (excluding Information Retrieval) in 2024. For each program that meets the distance requirements, please collect: 1) Complete university name, city, and ranking; 2) Shortest driving distance from the Natural History Museum of Los Angeles County (in miles, integers only); Please save the information as 'AI_univ_LA_500miles_Top30_2024.json' in the following format, sorting universities by distance from nearest to farthest, with higher-ranked universities listed first when distances are equal:

```
[ 
  { "university":"{name}", "city":"{city}", "cs_ranking_rank":{rank}, "car_drive_miles":{miles} }, 
  { "university":"{name}", "city":"{city}", "cs_ranking_rank":{rank}, "car_drive_miles":{miles} }, 
  ... 
]
```

  - generic [ref=e404]:
    - paragraph [ref=e405]:
      - text: This ranking is designed to identify institutions and faculty actively engaged in research across a number of areas of computer science, based on the number of publications by faculty that have appeared at the most selective conferences in each area of computer science (see the
      - link "FAQ" [ref=e408] [cursor=pointer]:
        - /url: faq.html
      - text: for more details).

<div className="thinking-box">
üßê`Agent`

Perfect! Now I have the AI rankings excluding Information Retrieval. I can see the top 30 universities in AI. Now I need to:

1. Set the date range to 2024 (currently it's 2015-2025)
2. Get the list of top 30 universities
3. Find their locations and calculate distances from Natural History Museum of Los Angeles County

  - generic [ref=e404]:
    - paragraph [ref=e405]:
      - text: This ranking is designed to identify institutions and faculty actively engaged in research across a number of areas of computer science, based on the number of publications by faculty that have appeared at the most selective conferences in each area of computer science (see the
      - link "FAQ" [ref=e408] [cursor=pointer]:
        - /url: faq.html
      - text: for more details).

    - paragraph [ref=e405]:
      - text: This ranking is designed to identify institutions and faculty actively engaged in research across a number of areas of computer science, based on the number of publications by faculty that have appeared at the most selective conferences in each area of computer science (see the
      - link "FAQ" [ref=e408] [cursor=pointer]:
        - /url: faq.html
      - text: for more details).

    - text: All publication data is from
    - link "DBLP" [ref=e434] [cursor=pointer]:
      - /url: https://dblp.org/
    - text: (updated quarterly; last update July 2025). Click to see
    - link "the current database of faculty and their affiliations" [ref=e435] [cursor=pointer]:
      - /url: https://github.com/emeryberger/CSrankings/blob/gh-pages/csrankings.csv
    - text: .
    - generic [ref=e436]:
      - text: Please submit any affiliation updates by editing the appropriate files and issuing a "pull request". Please verify that the faculty members are full-time, tenure-track faculty
      - emphasis [ref=e437]: who can solely advise a PhD student in Computer Science
      - text: ", and that their names are as they appear in DBLP."
    - text: "All code and data is available here:"
    - link "https://github.com/emeryberger/CSRankings" [ref=e438] [cursor=pointer]:

    - paragraph [ref=e405]:
      - text: This ranking is designed to identify institutions and faculty actively engaged in research across a number of areas of computer science, based on the number of publications by faculty that have appeared at the most selective conferences in each area of computer science (see the
      - link "FAQ" [ref=e408] [cursor=pointer]:
        - /url: faq.html
      - text: for more details).

    - text: All publication data is from
    - link "DBLP" [ref=e434] [cursor=pointer]:
      - /url: https://dblp.org/
    - text: (updated quarterly; last update July 2025). Click to see
    - link "the current database of faculty and their affiliations" [ref=e435] [cursor=pointer]:
      - /url: https://github.com/emeryberger/CSrankings/blob/gh-pages/csrankings.csv
    - text: .
    - generic [ref=e436]:
      - text: Please submit any affiliation updates by editing the appropriate files and issuing a "pull request". Please verify that the faculty members are full-time, tenure-track faculty
      - emphasis [ref=e437]: who can solely advise a PhD student in Computer Science
      - text: ", and that their names are as they appear in DBLP."
    - text: "All code and data is available here:"
    - link "https://github.com/emeryberger/CSRankings" [ref=e438] [cursor=pointer]:
